<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of <i>Adventure Time</i> episodes</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Adventure_Time_logo.png"><img alt="Adventure Time logo.png" data-file-height="198" data-file-width="501" height="87" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6f/Adventure_Time_logo.png/220px-Adventure_Time_logo.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6f/Adventure_Time_logo.png/330px-Adventure_Time_logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6f/Adventure_Time_logo.png/440px-Adventure_Time_logo.png 2x" width="220"/></a></div>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Adventure_Time" title="Adventure Time">Adventure Time</a></i> is an American animated television series created by <a href="/wiki/Pendleton_Ward" title="Pendleton Ward">Pendleton Ward</a> for <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network" title="Cartoon Network">Cartoon Network</a>. The series follows the adventures of <a href="/wiki/Finn_the_Human" title="Finn the Human">Finn</a> (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Shada" title="Jeremy Shada">Jeremy Shada</a>), a human boy, and his best friend and adoptive brother <a href="/wiki/Jake_the_Dog" title="Jake the Dog">Jake</a> (voiced by <a href="/wiki/John_DiMaggio" title="John DiMaggio">John DiMaggio</a>), a dog with magical powers to <a href="/wiki/Shapeshifting" title="Shapeshifting">change shape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Resizing_(fiction)" title="Resizing (fiction)">grow and shrink</a> at will. Finn and Jake live in the post-apocalyptic Land of Ooo. Throughout the series, they interact with the show's other main characters: <a href="/wiki/Princess_Bubblegum" title="Princess Bubblegum">Princess Bubblegum</a> (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Hynden_Walch" title="Hynden Walch">Hynden Walch</a>), the sovereign of the Candy Kingdom; the <a href="/wiki/Ice_King" title="Ice King">Ice King</a> (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Kenny" title="Tom Kenny">Tom Kenny</a>), a demented but largely misunderstood ice wizard; <a href="/wiki/Marceline_the_Vampire_Queen" title="Marceline the Vampire Queen">Marceline the Vampire Queen</a> (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Olivia_Olson" title="Olivia Olson">Olivia Olson</a>), a thousand-year-old vampire and <a href="/wiki/Rock_music" title="Rock music">rock music</a> enthusiast; and BMO (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Niki_Yang" title="Niki Yang">Niki Yang</a>), a sentient video game console-shaped <a href="/wiki/Robot" title="Robot">robot</a> that lives with Finn and Jake.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Adventure_Time_(pilot)" title="Adventure Time (pilot)">pilot</a> first aired in 2007,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-anotherera_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-anotherera-2">[2]</a></sup> and it was later re-aired on the incubator series <i><a href="/wiki/Random!_Cartoons" title="Random! Cartoons">Random! Cartoons</a></i> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nicktoons_Network" title="Nicktoons Network">Nicktoons Network</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timeenter_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-timeenter-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-episodecitepilot_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-episodecitepilot-4">[4]</a></sup> The pilot eventually leaked onto the internet and became a cult hit on <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Nickelodeon" title="Nickelodeon">Nickelodeon</a> declined to turn the short into a full-fledged show, Cartoon Network purchased the rights, and <i>Adventure Time</i> launched as a series on April 5, 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enchiridion_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-enchiridion-6">[6]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-season1airdate_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-season1airdate-7">[7]</a></sup> Season seven, which also contains a special mini-series, began airing on November 2, 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-seasonseven_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-seasonseven-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> The show has also been renewed for an <a href="/wiki/Adventure_Time_(season_8)" title="Adventure Time (season 8)">eighth season</a>, and a feature-length film—which is being developed by <a href="/wiki/Chris_McKay" title="Chris McKay">Chris McKay</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roy_Lee" title="Roy Lee">Roy Lee</a>—is also in the works.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-season8renewal_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-season8renewal-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></p>
<p>Each <i>Adventure Time</i> episode is about eleven minutes in length; pairs of episodes are often telecast in order to fill a half-hour program time slot.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> The first four seasons each contain 26 episodes, the fifth contains 52 episodes, the sixth contains 43 episodes, and the seventh contains 39. For the first five and a half seasons, the show aired on Monday nights.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[nb 1]</a></sup> However, starting with the sixth-season episode "Breezy", the show began to shift both its timeslot and its day of airing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[13]</a></sup> Ever since its debut, <i>Adventure Time</i> has been a ratings success for Cartoon Network, with the highest-rated episodes scoring over 3 million viewers. The show has received positive reviews from critics and has developed a strong following among teenagers and adults, many of whom are attracted due to the series' animation, stories, and characters.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[14]</a></sup> <i>Adventure Time</i> has won two <a href="/wiki/Annie_Award" title="Annie Award">Annie Awards</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[15]</a></sup> six <a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">Primetime Emmy Awards</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[16]</a></sup> two <a href="/wiki/British_Academy_Children%27s_Awards" title="British Academy Children's Awards">British Academy Children's Awards</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[18]</a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/Motion_Picture_Sound_Editors" title="Motion Picture Sound Editors">Motion Picture Sound Editors Award</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[19]</a></sup> a Pixel Award,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[20]</a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/Peabody_Award" title="Peabody Award">Peabody Award</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[21]</a></sup> and a <a href="/wiki/Kerrang!_Awards" title="Kerrang! Awards">Kerrang! Award</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[22]</a></sup> The series has also been nominated for three <a href="/wiki/Critics%27_Choice_Television_Award" title="Critics' Choice Television Award">Critics' Choice Television Awards</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[23]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[24]</a></sup> two <a href="/wiki/Annecy_International_Animated_Film_Festival" title="Annecy International Animated Film Festival">Annecy Festival Awards</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[25]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[26]</a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/TCA_Awards" title="TCA Awards">TCA Award</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-toonzonemarcyawards_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-toonzonemarcyawards-28">[27]</a></sup> and a <a href="/wiki/Sundance_Film_Festival" title="Sundance Film Festival">Sundance Film Festival Award</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[28]</a></sup> among others. Several compilation DVDs have been released. In addition, the first six seasons have been released on DVD and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blu-ray_Disc" title="Blu-ray Disc">Blu-ray</a>. <i>Adventure Time</i> is produced by <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network_Studios" title="Cartoon Network Studios">Cartoon Network Studios</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frederator_Studios" title="Frederator Studios">Frederator Studios</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".22Graybles_Allsorts.22_shorts">"Graybles Allsorts" shorts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Adventure_Time_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title='Edit section: "Graybles Allsorts" shorts'>edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".22Frog_Seasons.22_shorts">"Frog Seasons" shorts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Adventure_Time_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title='Edit section: "Frog Seasons" shorts'>edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Adventure_Time_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">An exception to this is the third season episode "Thank You" which aired on a Wednesday as a holiday special.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-33"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-33">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The pilot initially was aired as a stand-alone short on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nicktoons_(United_States)" title="Nicktoons (United States)">Nicktoons Network</a> January 11, 2007,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-anotherera_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-anotherera-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[31]</a></sup> before it was re-aired as part of the Nicktoons' series <i><a href="/wiki/Random!_Cartoons" title="Random! Cartoons">Random! Cartoons</a></i> on December 7, 2008.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-episodecitepilot_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-episodecitepilot-4">[4]</a></sup> As such, the original, stand-alone 2007 air date is included here.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-111"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-111">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Larry_Leichliter" title="Larry Leichliter">Larry Leichliter</a> served as director for the first part of the season, before the title was phased out solely in favor of "supervising director" and "art director".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-directorquestion_110-0"><a href="#cite_note-directorquestion-110">[108]</a></sup> For all episodes in season five (except "A Glitch is a Glitch"), <a href="/wiki/Nick_Jennings_(artist)" title="Nick Jennings (artist)">Nick Jennings</a> served as the art director. This column will therefore list either the episodes' directors and/or the different supervising directors.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-119"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-119">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">On the credit screen for the episode "Davey", it is stated that the episode was storyboarded by <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Moynihan" title="Jesse Moynihan">Jesse Moynihan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Skyler_Page" title="Skyler Page">Skyler Page</a>. However, this is erroneous, and the episode was actually storyboarded by Page and Somvilay Xayaphone, according to Pendleton Ward.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-whodidwhatdavey_118-0"><a href="#cite_note-whodidwhatdavey-118">[115]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-128"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-128">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">According to <a href="/wiki/Rebecca_Sugar" title="Rebecca Sugar">Rebecca Sugar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Adam_Muto" title="Adam Muto">Adam Muto</a> also contributed "additional scenes" to the episode and "did a lot on this one and put it over the top."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[123]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-171"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-171">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"Evergreen" first aired on November 10, 2014 on <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network_(Latin_America)" title="Cartoon Network (Latin America)">Cartoon Network</a> in Latin America.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-brazailairing_167-0"><a href="#cite_note-brazailairing-167">[162]</a></sup> "Astral Plane" was first uploaded on December 24, 2014 onto <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network_(Latin_America)" title="Cartoon Network (Latin America)">Cartoon Network</a>'s official Brazilian website.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-brazilupload_168-0"><a href="#cite_note-brazilupload-168">[163]</a></sup> "The Visitor" first aired on February 3, 2015 on <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network_(South_Korea)" title="Cartoon Network (South Korea)">Cartoon Network</a> in South Korea.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-koreaairing_169-0"><a href="#cite_note-koreaairing-169">[164]</a></sup> "Friends Forever" and "Jermaine" aired on <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network_(Latin_America)" title="Cartoon Network (Latin America)">Cartoon Network</a> in Latin America on April 6, 2015 and April 13, 2015 respectively.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-latinamerplots_170-0"><a href="#cite_note-latinamerplots-170">[165]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-237"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-237">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Seven minutes of this episode were animated and directed by Alex &amp; Lindsay Small-Butera.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-236"><a href="#cite_note-236">[230]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-2b-249"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2b_249-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">While the <i>Islands</i> miniseries aired on <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network" title="Cartoon Network">Cartoon Network</a> from January 30 until February 2, all the episodes were released on DVD and made available for download on <a href="/wiki/ITunes" title="ITunes">iTunes</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amazon.com" title="Amazon.com">Amazon.com</a> on January 24, 2017. However, because this field specifically refers to episode airdates, the information here regarding <i>Islands</i> will denote when the episodes first aired on Cartoon Network.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-248"><a href="#cite_note-248">[241]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-270"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-270">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wal-Mart" title="Wal-Mart">Wal-Mart</a> released a special, two-disc version of this DVD in October of 2012. This release added four new episodes (2 from season one, 1 from season two, and 1 from season four), bringing the run-time up to 176 minutes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-269"><a href="#cite_note-269">[261]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-295"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-295">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This DVD is not a complete season two release, as it omits "It Came from the Nightosphere", "Death in Bloom", "Mortal Folly", and "Mortal Recoil".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ukseason2dvd_294-1"><a href="#cite_note-ukseason2dvd-294">[285]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-297"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-297">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This DVD is not a complete season three release, as it omits "The Creeps", "From Bad to Worse", "No One Can Hear You", "Jake vs. Me-Mow", and "Ghost Princess".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ukseason2dvd_294-2"><a href="#cite_note-ukseason2dvd-294">[285]</a></sup></span></li>
</ol>
